 The method of telling long stories in Urdu is called Dastangoi
 hamanen bhi apni daadi-nani se kisse or kahaniyaan khub suunin
 Although it would be more appropriate to call it Kisasagoi instead of Dastangoi
 ham apane bujurgon se kahaniyaan sunate-sunate hi ludhak jaaya karte, magar bachapane main suni gai un kahaniyon kii yaad ab bhi dhundhlee nahin hui he
 We keep remembering those same stories again and again with our colleagues and juniors
 puraani kisse-kahaniyon ko kuredna hi to nostalgia he
 While this mode is on the verge of ending slowly on one side, on the other hand, some jawless people are trying to revive it
 is azim-o-shaan kala ne beete saal apane punarutthan ke das saal puure kar liye hai
 Where some young people are vigorously trying to restore this forgotten genre
 vahiin saamaanya jan bhi teji se is ore mude hai
 People are participating in such programs in large numbers and at the same time they are being well liked on mediums like youtube
 yahaan ham aapako phir se bataate chalem ki daastangoi urdu main daastaan yani lambii kahaniyaan sunaane kii kala he
 Alif Laila, Hatimatai and many other stories are heard in Urdu, but the most famous among them is 'dastane Amir Hamza', which contains the narration of Hazrat Mohammad's uncle Amir Hamza
 mughalon ke jamaane main hindustan ai ye kala 18veen or 19veen shatabdi main apane charam par thi
 In later years, it declined and with the arrival of the last Dastango Mir Bakar Ali in 1928, this art completely disappeared
 haalanki is vidha ko phir se jivit karne auraam avamke bich le jane kaa jimmaa mahmud faruki saab ne phir se uthaaya he
 They are working on it again
 is vidha main ab dhire-dhire mahilaayein bhi apane hunar kii aajamaaish kar rahi hai
 Mahakumbh of literature will be held in Delhi on 12-13, see full schedule
 Now you must be wondering why and why we are telling so much
 to ham bataa den ki desh kaa number ek khabariyaa channel aaj tak ek saahitiyik samagam karaane ja rahaa he

 pradesh ke charchit aiji amitabh thakur kii patni dow

 Lucknow has a total of 43 police stations, out of which 14 police stations are Kshatriyas, 11 are Brahmins, 9 are Other Backward Classes, 8 are Scheduled Castes and only 1 police station is appointed as General Muslim Police Station Incharge
 is prakaar lakhanu ke kul thana prabhariyon main 60 fisadi thana prabharee kshatriya yaa brahman jati ke hai, jisamen akele kshatriya jati ke ek-tihaai thana prabharee hai

 isamen unhone kaha ki aage se wo anushaasan main rahengi or pradhanmantri modi se milakar apni baat ko saaf bhi karengi
 Why Akash Vijayvargiya got the notice Last month, Akash Vijayvargiya, son of BJP national general secretary Kailash Vijayvargiya, beat a cricket bat of a municipal officer who had come to demolish a dilapidated building in Indore
 is ghatana ke tool pakadaney ke baad pradhanmantri narendra modi ne sakht rukh dikhaaya
 In the BJP parliamentary party meeting, Modi had said without naming Akash Vijayvargiya that it is not a tradition in our party to apply, plead again
 piem ne ye bhi kaha tha, 'chaahe kisi kaa bhi betaa hon hamen aise vidhayak kii jarurat nahin he, agar ek vidhayak kam bhi ho jaae to party koi fark nahin padataa he, jo sthaneey netaa us vidhayak ke jail se baahar aane par swaagat karne gaye unhen bhi party se nikaal dena chahie
 'on this matter, BJP gave a' show cause 'notice to Akash Vijayvargiya on 4 July
 unhen is notice kaa jawaab dene ke liye 15 din kaa vakt diya gaya
 Last week, Akash Vijayvargiya had apologized while replying to the notice
 is bich, somvaar ko bhi sadhvi pragna ko bijepi ke mahasachiv (sanghathan) biel santosh ne talab kiya
 Sadhvi Pragya reached the BJP office for this
 ek or bayaan se sadhvi pragna mushkil menhaal hi main sadhvi pragna kaa video soshal media par viral hua he jisamen wo kahati dikh rahi hai ki shauchalay yaa naaliyon kii safai karnaa unka kaam nahin hai or wo iske liye nahin chuni gai hai
 Sadhvi Pragya was also angry with the party for the statement of drains cleaning and was instructed not to make such statements in future
 philhal to nathuram godse ko deshbhakt bataane vaale bayaan par sadhvi pragna party kii ore se jari notice kaa jawaab de chuki hai, lekin party kii anushaasan samiti kii baithak nahin ho paane kii vajah se un par faisla adhar main lataka hua he
 According to the bjp's constitution, only the BJP Parliamentary Board has the right to take any action on any MP and MLA
 sutron ke mutabik abhi tak anushaasan samiti ne sadhvi pragna or akaash vijayawargeey ke maamalon main koi sanstuti nahin bheji he
 Sadhvi Pragya and Akash Vijayvargiya have undoubtedly responded to the notices on their own
 ab bada sawaal ye he ki anushaasan samiti unke javaabon se santusht hogi yaa phir koi karrwai kii sifarish karegi
 Everyone's eyes are on what the discipline committee takes on Sadhvi Pragya and Akash Vijayvargiya, because PM Modi does not comment on anyone

 shahrukh khan kii baaki filmon ke mukaable 'chennai express' kaa sangeet bhi saadhaaran he

 Google has recalled Sanford Fleming, the Canadian inventor who devised standard time for the world, by creating a doodle on his 190th birth anniversary
 vah scottish mul ke the
 Google said in its statement, "today's doodle reflects Fleming's legacy on his 190th birth anniversary
 " Fleming's train is believed to have been missed in Ireland due to the incorrect timetable being printed in 1876, after which he had the brilliant idea of devising standard time
 fleming kaa janm scotland ke karkaldi main 1827 main hua tha
 Fleming proposed Standard Time at a meeting of the Royal Canadian Institute on February 8, 1879
 unhone greenvich rekha se shuruyaat karte hue 15 degree ke antaraal sthaan par duniyabar ko 24 samay jones main vibhajit karne kii baat kahi
 Following his proposal, the 'international Prime Meridian Conference' was organized in 1884, covering 25 countries
 is sammelan main fleming kii antarrashtriya maanak samay pranali ko apanaaya gaya
 The comments fleming ne canada ke pacific railway main apane kaarykaal ke dauraan intercantinental railway ke nirmaan main bhi madad kii
 He is also known for designing Canada's first postage stamp
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) aisa mana jaataa he ki 1876 main galat samay saarini mudrit hone ke kaaran ireland main fleming kii train chhot gai thi, jiske baad unke man main maanak samay ijad karne kaa shandaar vichaar aayaa
 Fleming was born in 1827 in Carcaldi, Scotland
 fleming ne aath farvari 1879 ko royal canadian institute kii ek baithak main maanak samay kaa prastaav rakhaa tha
 He spoke of dividing the world into 24 time zones at an interval of 15 degrees, starting from the Greenwich line
 unke prastaav ke baad 1884 main 'international prime meridian conference' yojit kii gai, jisamen 25 desh shaamil hue
 The convention adopted Fleming's International Standard Time System
 tippaniyan Fleming also helped build the Intercontinental Railway during his tenure at Canadian Pacific Railway

 iske alaava or jaankaree nahin
 It is clear that there is no sign of free bicycle and free helmet distributors
 donon link ko clic karte hi ek pej khulata he
 At the top of the page is a picture of Prime Minister Narendra Modi, a picture of Ashok Chakra and then a picture of a bicycle / helmet
 in tasveeron ke thik neeche "pradhanmantri cycle yojana 2018" or "pradhanmantri sadak suraksha yojana" likhaa hua he
 For a bicycle, it is written on a pink strip that to get a free cycle, enter your name, your father's name, school name, class, your address and your state name

 iske thik baad ek vigyaapan kaa link

 is aavedan kii pushti ke liye neeche di gai prakriya ko puraa kare

 iske baad nile batan par clic kar apana order number praapt karen

 bas is tarah ke massej ko soshal media plateform par logon ko gumraah karne ke liye istemaal kiya ja rahaa he
 The purpose of these fake websites is to fill their pockets with advertisements appearing on the page
 bataa den ki pehle bhi ‘pradhanmantri free laptop yojana’ or ‘pradhanmantri free smartphone yojana’ jaise massej soshal media par failaae gaye the jo farji sabit hue the

 lekin logon ko khud bhi aise bhraamak massej se sajag rahanaa chahie

 aise main massej or unamem die gaye daavon kii khud bhi pehle padtaal karnaa aavashyak he

 02 lakh i-tikat book kiye
 Earlier on 4 July 7
 96 lakh i-tikat book kiye gaye the

 tippaniyan Recently IRCTC has increased the capacity of the website 3
 5 karod rupee tathaa software license tathaa storage aria network par 3 karod rupee kharch kiye hai

 purv main isamen dul kor sarwar (8jibi ram) laga tha

 company ke mutabik google ne 1
 Has acquired htc's mobile division team for $ 1 billion
 google kuch saalon se lagaataar apane hardware divijan par kaam kar rahaa he or iskaa behtareen udhaaharan pichley saal launch kiya gaya Pixel or Pixel XL smartphone he

 Google and HTC have been working together before, and htc's first Nexus device was also made by Google
 new york times ke mutabik achatisi ke siefo peter shen ne kaha he ki is deal ke baad bhi achatisi ke paas 2 hajaar se zyada research or dizin staff rahenge
 If you are wondering if htc's handset business will stop like blackberry, it is not so
 kyonki company ne saaf kaha he ki achatisi apane brands ke saath aage bhi kaam karti rahegi

 aapako bataa den ki mobile bijness main aane kaa plan google ne pehle bhi banaaya tha
 For this, the company acquired Motorola Mobility in 2011 for about 12
 5 billian dollar main kharida or kuch smartphone launch bhi kiye
 But later Motorola was sold again to Lenovo
 google or achatisi kii is deal kaa sidhaa asar smartfonindustry ko hoga

 kyonki achatisi smartphone kii team ab google ke paas hogi or ye ab milakar samsung or aipal ko takkar de sakate hai

 pichley chaar dinon se bijli hamase dur he
